In late mediaeval times, when it had become common in the West for priests to say Mass without the assistance of a choir and other ministers, these books began to be combined into a \"Mass book\" (missale in Latin), for the priest's use alone. This led to the appearance of the missale plenum (\"full or complete missal\"), which contained all the texts of the Mass, but without the music of the choir parts. Indications of the rubrics to be followed were also added.\r\n\r\nThe Roman Missal (Missale Romanum) published by Pope St. Pius V in 1570 eventually replaced the widespread use of different missal traditions by different parts of the church, such as those of Troyes, Sarum (Salisbury), and others. Many episcopal sees had in addition some local prayers and feast days.\r\n\r\nThe term \"missal\" is also used for books intended for use not by the priest but by others assisting at Mass. These books are sometimes referred to as \"hand missals\" or \"missalettes\", while the term \"altar missal\" is sometimes used to distinguish the missal for the priest's use from them. Usually they omit or severely abbreviate the rubrical portions and Mass texts for other than the regular yearly celebrations, but include the Scripture readings.","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9NBLGGH35HWM","TileLayout":"Square","Title":"Smarty CRM Agenda","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"logo","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.54914.13510798885201734.d7179d85-d90f-4edc-ac87-8ab34620ee18.ba6bf752-d77f-404d-bb05-e31cde69453e","Height":300,"Width":300,"BackgroundColor":"","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"Gratis⁺","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":0.0,"RatingsCount":"0","PackageFamilyNames":["CloudsTechnologiesLLC.SmartyCRM_gcf1ga05yynet"],"ContentIds":["6c59e64a-e856-ed02-2e90-f6e25c630051","a3dde225-47c7-0166-cf80-b56c7a4ff6db"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"PC","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Web version: https://smartycrm.com.\r\n\r\nSmarty CRM es un organizador para uso diario.\r\nAhora siempre tendrás a mano las herramientas siguientes:\r\n\r\ncontactos;\r\nnotas;\r\nproyectos y tareas;\r\nagenda, etc.\r\n\r\nSmarty CRM es una gran solución para empresas.\r\nEl servicio está diseñado para gestionar todos los procesos de negocio de la empresa.
